  <script type="text/javascript">
      (function() {
          var errCount = 10;
          function sendErrorToServer(level, data) {
              data.userAgent = window.navigator && window.navigator.userAgent;
              var body = JSON.stringify(data);

              if (errCount > 0) {
                  errCount--;
                  var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
                  xhr.open('POST', '/jserror/' + level);
                  xhr.timeout = 1000;
                  xhr.send(body);
                  if (errCount <= 0) { setTimeout(function() {errCount = 10}, 300000);}
              }
          }
          window.logger = {
              error: function (data) {
                  sendErrorToServer('error', data);
              },
              warn: function (data) {
                  sendErrorToServer('warn', data);
              },
              info: function (data) {
                  sendErrorToServer('info', data);
              }
          };
          function onError(message, scriptUrl, line, column, error) {
              if (message && typeof message !== 'string' && message.type && message.target) {
                  var event = message;
                  try {
                      error = event.error;
                      line = event.lineno;
                      column = event.colno;
                      scriptUrl = event.target && event.target.src || undefined;
                      message = event.message;
                  } catch (e) {}
              }
              var stack = error && error.stack;
              if (stack) {
                  stack = stack.split('\n');
              }
              if (!stack) {
                  stack = scriptUrl ? 'file: ' + scriptUrl + ':' + line + ':' + column : 'nofile';
              }
              window.logger.error({
                  name: 'Browser error:' + (error && error.name || 'Error'),
                  message,
                  stack: stack,
                  details: error && error.details
              });
          }
          window.addEventListener('error', onError);
      })();
  </script>
